// it will be copied here.\\n80:     borrow(ref_to_val);\\n81: }\\n82: ```\\n83: \\n84: For more information on Rust's ownership system, take a look at the\\n85: [References & Borrowing][references-and-borrowing] section of the Book.\\n86: \\n87: [references-and-borrowing]: https://doc.rust-lang.org/book/ch04-02-references-and-borrowing.html\\n88: \",\"url\":\"https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/github.com/sg-evals/rust--01f6ddf7@525258043d7f9dcc1b69d9abcb9bfea32826a219/-/blob/compiler/rustc_error_codes/src/error_codes/E0505.md\"}","structuredContent":{"content":"1: A value was moved out while it was still borrowed.\n2: \n3: Erroneous code example:\n4: \n5: ```compile_fail,E0505\n6: struct Value {}\n7: \n8: fn borrow(val: &Value) {}\n9: \n10: fn eat(val: Value) {}\n11: \n12: fn main() {\n13:     let x = Value{};\n14:     let _ref_to_val: &Value = &x;\n15:     eat(x);\n16:     borrow(_ref_to_val);\n17: }\n18: ```\n19: \n20: Here, the function `eat` takes ownership of `x`. However,\n21: `x` cannot be moved because the borrow to `_ref_to_val`\n22: needs to last till the function `borrow`.\n23: To fix that you can do a few different things:\n24: \n25: * Try to avoid moving the variable.\n26: * Release borrow before move.\n27: * Implement the `Copy` trait on the type.\n28: \n29: Examples:\n30: \n31: ```\n32: struct Value {}\n33: \n34: fn borrow(val: &Value) {}\n35: \n36: fn eat(val: &Value) {}\n37: \n38: fn main() {\n39:     let x = Value{};\n40: \n41:     let ref_to_val: &Value = &x;\n42:     eat(&x); // pass by reference, if it's possible\n43:     borrow(ref_to_val);\n44: }\n45: ```\n46: \n47: Or:\n48: \n49: ```\n50: struct Value {}\n51: \n52: fn borrow(val: &Value) {}\n53: \n54: fn eat(val: Value) {}\n55: \n56: fn main() {\n57:     let x = Value{};\n58: \n59:     let ref_to_val: &Value = &x;\n60:     borrow(ref_to_val);\n61:     // ref_to_val is no longer used.\n62:     eat(x);\n63: }\n64: ```\n65: \n66: Or:\n67: \n68: ```\n69: #[derive(Clone, Copy)] // implement Copy trait\n70: struct Value {}\n71: \n72: fn borrow(val: &Value) {}\n73: \n74: fn eat(val: Value) {}\n75: \n76: fn main() {\n77:     let x = Value{};\n78:     let ref_to_val: &Value = &x;\n79:     eat(x); // it will be copied here.\n80:     borrow(ref_to_val);\n81: }\n82: ```\n83: \n84: For more information on Rust's ownership system, take a look at the\n85: [References & Borrowing][references-and-borrowing] section of the Book.\n86: \n87: [references-and-borrowing]: https://doc.rust-lang.org/book/ch04-02-references-and-borrowing.html\n88: ","url":"https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/github.com/sg-evals/rust--01f6ddf7@525258043d7f9dcc1b69d9abcb9bfea32826a219/-/blob/compiler/rustc_error_codes/src/error_codes/E0505.md"}}}

Similar to `typeck`, this must\n115: /// only be called for typeck roots which will then borrowck all\n116: /// nested bodies as well.\n117: fn mir_borrowck(\n118:     tcx: TyCtxt<'_>,\n119:     def: LocalDefId,\n120: ) -> Result<&FxIndexMap<LocalDefId, ty::DefinitionSiteHiddenType<'_>>, ErrorGuaranteed> {\n121:     assert!(!tcx.is_typeck_child(def.to_def_id()));\n122:     let (input_body, _) = tcx.mir_promoted(def);\n123:     debug!(\"run query mir_borrowck: {}\", tcx.def_path_str(def));\n124: \n125:     let input_body: &Body<'_> = &input_body.borrow();\n126:     if let Some(guar) = input_body.tainted_by_errors {\n127:         debug!(\"Skipping borrowck because of tainted body\");\n128:         Err(guar)\n129:     } else if input_body.should_skip() {\n130:         debug!(\"Skipping borrowck because of injected body\");\n131:         let opaque_types = Default::default();\n132:         Ok(tcx.arena.alloc(opaque_types))\n133:     } else {\n134:         let mut root_cx = BorrowCheckRootCtxt::new(tcx, def, None);\n135:         root_cx.do_mir_borrowck();\n136:         root_cx.finalize()\n137:     }\n138: }\n139: \n140: /// Data propagated to the typeck parent by nested items.\n141: /// This should always be empty for the typeck root.\n142: #[derive(Debug)]\n143: struct PropagatedBorrowCheckResults<'tcx> {\n144:     closure_requirements: Option<ClosureRegionRequirements<'tcx>>,\n145:     used_mut_upvars: SmallVec<[FieldIdx; 8]>,\n146: }\n147: \n148: type DeferredClosureRequirements<'tcx> = Vec<(LocalDefId, ty::GenericArgsRef<'tcx>, Locations)>;\n149: \n150: /// After we borrow check a closure, we are left with various\n151: ","url":"https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/github.com/sg-evals/rust--01f6ddf7@525258043d7f9dcc1b69d9abcb9bfea32826a219/-/blob/compiler/rustc_borrowck/src/lib.rs%3FL1-150"}}}
